##### **ReasoningFlow: Discourse Structures for Understanding LLM Reasoning Traces**
2606.05402v1 by Jinu Lee, Shivam Agarwal, Amruta Parulekar, Siddarth Madala, Dilek Hakkani-Tur, Julia Hockenmaier

Large reasoning models (LRMs) produce reasoning traces with non-linear structures, such as backtracking and self-correction, that complicate the evaluation and monitoring of the reasoning process. We introduce ReasoningFlow, a framework that captures the discourse structures of LRM reasoning traces into fine-grained directed acyclic graphs (DAGs). We develop and validate our annotation schema through careful manual annotation of 31 traces (2.1k steps), achieving high inter-annotator agreement, then scale to automatic annotation of 1,260 traces (247.7k steps) spanning three tasks (math, science, argumentation) and five models (Qwen2.5-32B-Inst, QwQ-32B, DeepSeek-V3, DeepSeek-R1, GPT-oss-120B). By analyzing ReasoningFlow graphs, we find: (1) LRMs exhibit structurally similar traces, despite being trained from different base models and potentially non-overlapping post-training data. (2) ReasoningFlow reveals diverse fine-grained reasoning behaviors (e.g., local verification, self-reflection, and assumptions) that can be used for better reasoning trace monitorability. (3) In LRMs, most of the erroneous steps are not used to derive final answers. (4) Mechanistic causal dependencies between steps do not reflect the language-level discourse structure. We release the dataset and code in: https://github.com/jinulee-v/reasoningflow.

摘要：大型推理模型（LRMs）產生具有非線性結構的推理痕跡，例如回溯和自我修正，這使得推理過程的評估和監控變得複雜。我們引入了 ReasoningFlow，一個將 LRM 推理痕跡的話語結構捕捉為細粒度有向無循環圖（DAGs）的框架。我們通過對 31 條痕跡（2.1k 步驟）進行仔細的手動標註來開發和驗證我們的標註方案，達到高的標註者間一致性，然後擴展到對 1,260 條痕跡（247.7k 步驟）的自動標註，涵蓋三個任務（數學、科學、論證）和五個模型（Qwen2.5-32B-Inst、QwQ-32B、DeepSeek-V3、DeepSeek-R1、GPT-oss-120B）。通過分析 ReasoningFlow 圖，我們發現：（1）儘管是從不同的基礎模型訓練而來，且可能使用了不重疊的後訓練數據，LRMs 仍然表現出結構上相似的痕跡。（2）ReasoningFlow 揭示了多樣的細粒度推理行為（例如，本地驗證、自我反思和假設），可用於更好的推理痕跡監控。（3）在 LRMs 中，大多數錯誤步驟並未用於推導最終答案。（4）步驟之間的機械因果依賴關係並不反映語言層面的話語結構。我們在以下網址發布數據集和代碼：https://github.com/jinulee-v/reasoningflow。

##### **Attention Consistent Longitudinal Medical Visual Question Answering Guided by Vision Foundation Models**
2606.06534v1 by Jialin Wu, Qianru Zhang, Georges El Fakhri, Xiaofeng Liu

Longitudinal medical visual question answering (VQA) requires reasoning about anatomical differences between an image of a current time point and an image of a referred time point. We propose an attention-guided encoder-decoder for this task with chest X-rays. Instead of conventional direct contrast, we propose to include a lightweight affine registration module to reduce nuisance motion by co-registering the current image to the reference image with a small registration regularizer. The registered image pair is fed into the image encoder, followed by a frozen DINO-based mask generator and a trainable adaptive mask generator to produce masks applied to the original image pairs. The masked image pairs are again fed into the image encoder and concatenated with text features as the input to a multimodal transformer-based decoder to generate final answers. To facilitate learning stabilization and clarify the change signal, inspired by DINO-v3, we include additional auxiliary objectives, including a mask rebuilding loss, a pairwise Gram-style consistency loss, and a KoLeo uniformity loss, which enhances the geometry of the representation. On the Medical-Diff-VQA benchmark, the model delivers strong BLEU, ROUGE-L, CIDEr, and METEOR scores while offering intrinsic interpretability through the shared saliency mask. These results support saliency-conditioned generation with mild pre-alignment as a principled framework for longitudinal reasoning in medical VQA. Our training strategy also illustrates the potential of a paradigm in utilizing image foundation models in biomedicine: optimizing both supervised and unsupervised learning objectives simultaneously.

摘要：長期醫學視覺問題回答（VQA）需要推理當前時間點的影像與參考時間點影像之間的解剖差異。我們針對這一任務提出了一個基於注意力引導的編碼器-解碼器，使用胸部X光片。與傳統的直接對比不同，我們提議加入一個輕量級的仿射註冊模塊，通過使用小的註冊正則化器將當前影像與參考影像共同註冊，以減少干擾運動。註冊後的影像對被輸入到影像編碼器，接著是凍結的基於DINO的掩碼生成器和可訓練的自適應掩碼生成器，以生成應用於原始影像對的掩碼。掩碼影像對再次被輸入到影像編碼器，並與文本特徵拼接，作為多模態Transformer基礎的解碼器的輸入，以生成最終答案。為了促進學習穩定性並明確變化信號，受到DINO-v3的啟發，我們加入了額外的輔助目標，包括掩碼重建損失、一對一的Gram風格一致性損失和KoLeo均勻性損失，這增強了表示的幾何性。在Medical-Diff-VQA基準上，該模型提供了強大的BLEU、ROUGE-L、CIDEr和METEOR分數，同時通過共享的顯著性掩碼提供內在的可解釋性。這些結果支持在醫學VQA中使用輕微預對齊的顯著性條件生成作為長期推理的原則性框架。我們的訓練策略還展示了在生物醫學中利用影像基礎模型的潛力：同時優化監督和非監督學習目標。

##### **Who Needs Labels? Adapting Vision Foundation Models With the Metadata You Already Have**
2606.05107v1 by Elouan Gardès, Seung Eun Yi, Kartik Ahuja, Théo Moutakanni, Huy V. Vo, Piotr Bojanowski, Wolfgang M. Pernice, Loïc Landrieu, Camille Couprie

We propose a label-free approach to adapt powerful but generic vision foundation models to specialized scientific domains. Standard supervised fine-tuning is often ill-suited to these settings: labels are scarce, and task-specific training can collapse the model's generality and hurt robustness. We instead leverage metadata to adapt representations to new domains in a self-supervised manner. Our method, FINO, combines a standard self-supervised objective with flexible metadata guidance that handles both highly granular discrete metadata and continuous metadata. It encourages the representation to preserve informative factors while suppressing spurious ones. Across subcellular fluorescence microscopy, Earth observation, wildlife monitoring, and medical imaging, FINO consistently outperforms standard unsupervised domain adaptation and fully supervised adaptation. It also exceeds highly-specialized domain-specific state of the art, while using no task labels for backbone adaptation and only lightweight probes for supervision.

摘要：我們提出了一種無標籤的方法，以將強大但通用的視覺基礎模型適應於專門的科學領域。標準的監督微調通常不適合這些環境：標籤稀缺，且特定任務的訓練可能會削弱模型的通用性並損害穩健性。我們則利用元數據以自我監督的方式將表示適應到新領域。我們的方法FINO結合了標準的自我監督目標和靈活的元數據指導，能夠處理高度細化的離散元數據和連續元數據。它鼓勵表示保留信息因素，同時抑制虛假因素。在亞細胞熒光顯微鏡、地球觀測、野生動物監測和醫學影像等領域，FINO始終優於標準的無監督領域適應和完全監督的適應。它還超越了高度專業化的領域特定最先進技術，同時在骨幹適應中不使用任務標籤，並僅使用輕量級探針進行監督。

##### **Geometry-Aware Distillation for Prompt Tuning Biomedical Vision-Language Models**
2606.04922v1 by Tran Dinh Tien, Zhiqiang Shen

Current prompt-based and adapter-based tuning of vision-language models (VLMs) is attractive for medical imaging, where clinical data sensitivity favors frozen backbones and annotations are limited. However, these methods typically optimize only the ground-truth class, treating all other classes as equally incorrect, ignoring clinically meaningful class relations and yielding unstable decision boundaries in limited-supervision settings. We propose Omni-Geometry Knowledge Distillation (OGKD), a new framework that injects class-relation structure into the teacher to produce directional targets that preserve the ground truth while respecting inter-class geometry. Using these targets, we develop two distillation losses: Global Geometry-Aware Distillation (GAD) operates on the global image token, and Label-Guided Geometry Distillation (LGD) applies the same geometry to attentive patch tokens to improve fine-grained alignment. Across comprehensive experiments and analyses on 11 widely-used medical datasets for base-to-novel and few-shot evaluations, our OGKD achieves substantially better performance, consistently improving accuracy by an average absolute gain of 1.7%-2.8% over all prior state-of-the-art VLM adaptation counterparts. It also robustly generalizes to unseen classes and yields more reliable predictions than other approaches. Our code is available at https://github.com/tientrandinh/OGKD.

摘要：目前基於提示和適配器的視覺-語言模型 (VLMs) 調整在醫學影像中具有吸引力，因為臨床數據的敏感性偏好於固定的基礎架構，且註釋有限。<lb/>然而，這些方法通常僅優化真實類別，將所有其他類別視為同樣不正確，忽略臨床上有意義的類別關係，並在有限監督的環境中產生不穩定的決策邊界。<lb/>我們提出了全方位幾何知識蒸餾 (OGKD)，這是一個新的框架，將類別關係結構注入教師中，以產生保留真實值的方向性目標，同時尊重類別間的幾何關係。<lb/>利用這些目標，我們開發了兩種蒸餾損失：全球幾何感知蒸餾 (GAD) 在全球影像標記上運作，而標籤引導幾何蒸餾 (LGD) 將相同的幾何應用於關注的補丁標記，以改善細粒度對齊。<lb/>在針對11個廣泛使用的醫學數據集進行的全面實驗和分析中，我們的OGKD在基礎到新穎和少量樣本評估中達到了顯著更好的性能，平均絕對增益為1.7%-2.8%，持續提高準確性，超越所有先前的最先進VLM適應對手。<lb/>它還能穩健地推廣到未見過的類別，並比其他方法產生更可靠的預測。<lb/>我們的代碼可在 https://github.com/tientrandinh/OGKD 獲得。

##### **Enhancing MedSAM with a Lightweight Box Predictor for Medical Image Segmentation**
2606.04705v1 by Amirhossein Movahedisefat, Amirreza Fateh, Mohammad Reza Mohammadi

Semantic segmentation in medical imaging is a critical yet challenging task due to data scarcity and high variability across modalities. While foundation models like the Segment Anything Model (SAM) show promise, they often struggle with medical images without specific adaptation. Moreover, point prompts, despite being the most natural form of user interaction, provide insufficient spatial context for reliable segmentation, particularly when target structures are irregular or poorly contrasted. In this paper, we propose an enhanced segmentation framework that integrates a lightweight Box Predictor module into the MedSAM architecture. The Box Predictor estimates an approximate bounding box from a single user click using localized image embedding features, providing spatial guidance that reduces the ambiguity of point prompts, while introducing only 1.6M additional parameters and negligible inference overhead. We introduce a two-stage training pipeline where the Box Predictor is trained independently before being integrated into MedSAM. To validate the generalization capability of our method, we conduct extensive evaluations on four diverse datasets (FLARE22, BRISC, BUSI, LungSegDB) spanning distinct imaging modalities, including CT, MRI, and Ultrasound. Our method improves segmentation accuracy and robustness across varied anatomical structures and imaging domains, achieving Dice scores of 0.89 (BUSI), 0.93 (FLARE22), 0.88 (BRISC), and 0.98 (LungSegDB). Code is available at https://github.com/Amirhosseinmovahedi/MedSAM-BoxPredictor

摘要：醫學影像中的語意分割是一項關鍵但具有挑戰性的任務，因為數據稀缺且不同模態之間變異性高。雖然像Segment Anything Model (SAM)這樣的基礎模型顯示出潛力，但它們在沒有特定適應的情況下，往往難以處理醫學影像。此外，點提示儘管是最自然的用戶互動形式，但對於可靠的分割來說提供的空間上下文不足，特別是在目標結構不規則或對比度較差的情況下。在本文中，我們提出了一個增強的分割框架，將輕量級的Box Predictor模塊整合到MedSAM架構中。Box Predictor利用局部圖像嵌入特徵從單個用戶點擊估計近似邊界框，提供空間指導，減少點提示的模糊性，同時僅引入1.6M的額外參數和微不足道的推理開銷。我們引入了一個兩階段的訓練流程，其中Box Predictor在整合到MedSAM之前獨立訓練。為了驗證我們方法的泛化能力，我們在四個不同數據集（FLARE22、BRISC、BUSI、LungSegDB）上進行了廣泛評估，這些數據集涵蓋了不同的影像模態，包括CT、MRI和超聲。我們的方法提高了各種解剖結構和影像領域的分割準確性和穩健性，達到了0.89（BUSI）、0.93（FLARE22）、0.88（BRISC）和0.98（LungSegDB）的Dice分數。代碼可在https://github.com/Amirhosseinmovahedi/MedSAM-BoxPredictor獲得。

##### **Neetyabhas: A Framework for Uncertainty-Aware Public Policy Optimization in Rational Agent-Based Models**
2606.04562v1 by Janani Venugopalan, Gaurav Deshkar, Rishabh Gaur, Harshal Hayatnagarkar, Jayanta Kshirsagar

Purpose The WHO's COVID-19 non-pharmaceutical interventions (e.g., lockdowns, vaccinations) effectively curb transmission but impose heavy economic strains. Existing research often neglects individual behaviors and falsely assumes perfect infection tracking and flawless policy execution, failing to account for real-world uncertainties and errors. Methods We propose an integrative approach incorporating uncertainties in both epidemic measurement (infections/hospitalizations) and policy implementation. We built a simulation model of 1,000 individuals making real-time choices regarding mask-wearing, vaccination, and shopping. Concurrently, policymakers deploy interventions (lockdowns, mandates) based on health and economic observations. This framework is driven by hierarchical reinforcement learning agents, utilizing deep Q-networks alongside uncertainty-aware policy gradient variants (DDPG and TD3). Results The simulations effectively managed the epidemic's progression. Masking and vaccinations proved highly effective, significantly reducing both the outbreak's peak height and duration. By integrating individual behaviors, policy uncertainties, and multifaceted interventions, our dynamic control approach successfully mitigated the epidemic's impact. Conclusions Our model overcomes previous research limitations by embedding uncertainty and human behavior into public health policy frameworks. The simulation demonstrates that accounting for individual choices and imperfect data is crucial for designing effective interventions during complex pandemics, with masks and vaccines serving as pivotal tools.

摘要：目的 世界衛生組織的 COVID-19 非藥物干預措施（例如，封鎖、疫苗接種）有效地抑制了傳播，但對經濟造成了沉重的壓力。現有研究常常忽視個體行為，並錯誤地假設感染追蹤和政策執行是完美的，未能考慮現實世界中的不確定性和錯誤。方法 我們提出了一種綜合方法，將流行病測量（感染/住院）和政策執行中的不確定性納入考量。我們建立了一個模擬模型，包含 1,000 名個體，實時做出有關佩戴口罩、疫苗接種和購物的選擇。同時，政策制定者根據健康和經濟觀察部署干預措施（封鎖、命令）。這一框架由層級強化學習代理驅動，利用深度 Q 網絡和不確定性感知的政策梯度變體（DDPG 和 TD3）。結果 模擬有效管理了流行病的進展。佩戴口罩和疫苗接種被證明非常有效，顯著降低了疫情的高峰高度和持續時間。通過整合個體行為、政策不確定性和多方面的干預，我們的動態控制方法成功減輕了疫情的影響。結論 我們的模型通過將不確定性和人類行為嵌入公共衛生政策框架，克服了以往研究的限制。模擬顯示，考慮個體選擇和不完美數據對於在複雜疫情期間設計有效的干預措施至關重要，口罩和疫苗作為關鍵工具。

##### **TD-Grokking: Learning from Zero-Reward Problems by Training-Time Decomposition**
2606.09883v1 by Ningyuan Xi, Hao Xu, Hongsheng Xin, Ning Miao

Large language models (LLMs) have made remarkable progress in reasoning tasks, largely driven by post-training paradigms, especially reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). However, a critical bottleneck persists: RLVR fails on highly challenging zero-reward problems, where all sampled reasoning trajectories yield uniformly failed outcomes, providing no optimization signal to drive model improvement. Prior efforts to address this limitation, such as dense process supervision, partial reward assignment, or prefix-guided exploration, suffer from inherent task constraints or do not fully equip the policy model with the capabilities necessary to solve the original intractable problems. To address this, we propose TD-Grokking, a training-time decomposition framework for zero-reward problems. It recursively decomposes intractable root problems into self-contained, verifiable subproblems, forming hierarchical trees where solvable leaves provide non-zero rewards. Evaluations on mathematical and medical tasks show that TD-Grokking outperforms vanilla GRPO as well as all baseline approaches. Together with detailed analysis, these results confirm that training-time decomposition effectively converts zero-reward examples into usable training signals, enabling consistent performance gains. Our code and datasets are available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/TD-Grokking-6567/.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在推理任務上取得了顯著進展，這主要得益於後訓練範式，特別是具有可驗證獎勵的強化學習（RLVR）。然而，一個關鍵瓶頸依然存在：RLVR在高度挑戰性的零獎勵問題上失效，所有抽樣的推理軌跡都產生一致失敗的結果，無法提供優化信號以推動模型改進。之前為了解決這一限制所做的努力，例如密集過程監督、部分獎勵分配或前綴引導探索，均受到內在任務約束的影響，或者未能充分賦予策略模型解決原始難題所需的能力。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了TD-Grokking，這是一個針對零獎勵問題的訓練時分解框架。它將難以處理的根問題遞歸地分解為自包含的、可驗證的子問題，形成層次樹，其中可解的葉子提供非零獎勵。對數學和醫學任務的評估顯示，TD-Grokking的表現超過了普通的GRPO以及所有基準方法。結合詳細的分析，這些結果確認訓練時分解有效地將零獎勵示例轉化為可用的訓練信號，從而實現穩定的性能提升。我們的代碼和數據集可在 https://anonymous.4open.science/r/TD-Grokking-6567/ 獲得。

##### **Multi-Granularity 3D Kidney Lesion Characterization from CT Volumes**
2606.04365v1 by Renjie Liang, Zhengkang Fan, Jinqian Pan, Chenkun Sun, Jiang Bian, Russell Terry, Jie Xu

Radiology reports describe kidney lesions by type, size, enhancement, and attenuation, yet existing 3D methods predict only at the patient or organ level. We reformulate kidney CT characterization as a per-lesion set-prediction task: one model emits a variable number of lesions per kidney, each with four clinical attributes. We curated 2,619 CT volumes from 788 patients at one academic medical center, with multi-granularity side- and per-lesion labels, and used KiTS23 (489 cases) for zero-shot external validation. We propose \textbf{LesionDETR}, a DETR-style architecture with size-distance Hungarian matching and a hierarchical loss that aggregates per-slot outputs to side-level objectives. Across four input representations and six encoder initializations, two design choices dominate: a segmentation mask as an input channel, and same-domain abdominal pretraining (SuPreM); generic large-corpus pretraining is no better than random initialization. LesionDETR reaches bilateral side-level abnormality AUC $0.799 \pm 0.009$ on UF-Health and $0.817 \pm 0.072$ on KiTS23. A count-conditioned variant reaches per-lesion mAP $0.190 \pm 0.083$ on cystic lesions; rare solid-lesion AP stays at the noise floor, pointing to targeted data collection, not architecture, as the next bottleneck. The framework yields verified per-lesion predictions for downstream structured report generation.

摘要：放射科報告根據類型、大小、增強和衰減來描述腎臟病變，但現有的3D方法僅在患者或器官層面進行預測。我們將腎臟CT特徵化重新構造為每個病變的集合預測任務：一個模型為每個腎臟輸出可變數量的病變，每個病變具有四個臨床屬性。我們從一個學術醫療中心整理了2,619個CT影像，來自788名患者，並具有多粒度的側面和每個病變標籤，並使用KiTS23（489例）進行零樣本外部驗證。我們提出了\textbf{LesionDETR}，這是一種DETR風格的架構，具有大小-距離匈牙利匹配和一種層次損失，將每個槽的輸出聚合到側面級目標。在四種輸入表示和六種編碼器初始化中，兩個設計選擇佔主導地位：作為輸入通道的分割掩碼，以及同域腹部預訓練（SuPreM）；通用大型語料庫的預訓練不比隨機初始化好。LesionDETR在UF-Health上達到雙邊側面級異常AUC $0.799 \pm 0.009$，在KiTS23上達到$0.817 \pm 0.072$。一個基於計數的變體在囊性病變上達到每個病變的mAP $0.190 \pm 0.083$；稀有實體病變的AP保持在噪聲底線，指出針對性數據收集，而非架構，將是下一個瓶頸。該框架產生經過驗證的每個病變預測，用於下游結構化報告生成。

##### **Can I Take Another Dose? Evaluating LLM Decision-Making Under Temporal Uncertainty in OTC Dosing QA**
2606.04262v1 by Maroof Kousar, Yibo Hu

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for everyday health questions, including whether a user can safely take another dose of an over-the-counter (OTC) medication. Yet this common safety-relevant setting remains underexplored in existing medical QA evaluations, where correct answers require tracking dose timing, computing rolling 24-hour intake, following product-label constraints, and handling incomplete medication histories. We introduce DOSEBENCH, a focused benchmark of 81 curated OTC dosing scenarios focused on adult acetaminophen and ibuprofen use, with manually annotated gold references. We evaluate four LLMs across repeated runs using metrics for decision correctness, consistency, explanation verifiability, failure types, and confidence-related signals, resulting in 1,620 model responses. Our results show that models frequently struggle with rolling-window reasoning and ambiguity-sensitive cases and that stable or confident-looking responses can still violate dosing constraints. These findings suggest that OTC dosing QA provides a narrow yet practical testbed for evaluating temporal reasoning, constraint following, and safety-relevant uncertainty handling in medical QA.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地用於日常健康問題，包括用戶是否可以安全地服用另一劑非處方藥（OTC）。<lb/>然而，這個常見的安全相關場景在現有的醫療問答評估中仍然未受到充分探索，正確的答案需要追蹤劑量時間、計算滾動的24小時攝取量、遵循產品標籤的限制，並處理不完整的用藥歷史。<lb/>我們介紹了DOSEBENCH，一個專注於81個精心策劃的OTC劑量場景的基準，重點關注成人對乙醯氨基酚和布洛芬的使用，並附有手動標註的金標準參考。<lb/>我們在重複運行中評估了四個LLMs，使用決策正確性、一致性、解釋可驗證性、失敗類型和信心相關信號的指標，總共產生了1,620個模型回應。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，模型在滾動窗口推理和對模糊情況的敏感性方面經常遇到困難，而穩定或看起來自信的回應仍然可能違反劑量限制。<lb/>這些發現表明，OTC劑量問答提供了一個狹窄但實用的測試平台，用於評估醫療問答中的時間推理、約束遵循和安全相關的不確定性處理。

##### **The Differentiable Auditory Loop (DAL): An ML Framework for Hyper-Personalized Hearing Aids**
2606.04103v1 by Alejandro Ballesta Rosen, Jason Mikiel-Hunter, Julian Maclaren, Jack Collins, Richard F. Lyon, Simon Carlile

Conventional hearing aids rely on fixed, frequency-dependent amplification and compression to manage reduced sensitivity, which often fails to provide sufficient listening support in complex environments, such as situations with multiple speakers (the ``cocktail party'' problem). To more comprehensively address the underlying encoding dysfunctions of hearing loss, we introduce the Differentiable Auditory Loop (DAL), a new open-source framework for personalized hearing aid design and fitting. Our first implementation of DAL incorporates CARFAC, a differentiable model of human cochlear function, which we ported to JAX, to optimize a deep neural network to match impaired auditory neural activity patterns with a normal-hearing reference. To build a hearing aid with the fine-grained spectro-temporal signal processing required, we adopt SEANet, a waveform-to-waveform fully convolutional UNet generator. We fine-tune the network by comparing the outputs of a CARFAC model fitted to normal hearing with that of a CARFAC model fitted to match each subject's individual hearing impairment. The comparison is done using loss functions derived from the respective CARFAC neural activity pattern (NAP) outputs and stabilized auditory images (SAIs), the latter providing a 2D representation that captures phase-insensitive temporal structure in the auditory nerve output. Through gradient descent, the SEANet model learns to both denoise the input and compensate for the hearing loss modelled by the impaired CARFAC model. Across neural-representation and signal-fidelity metrics, the DAL-optimized SEANet model outperformed the tested master hearing aid (MHA) baselines. The DAL framework provides a practical path toward model-based, machine-learning-driven personalization of hearing aid signal processing. Next steps include hardware deployment to enable real-world clinical testing.

摘要：傳統的助聽器依賴固定的、頻率依賴的增益和壓縮來管理靈敏度降低，但在複雜環境中，如多位講者的情況（即“雞尾酒會”問題），這通常無法提供足夠的聽力支持。為了更全面地解決聽力損失的基本編碼功能障礙，我們引入了可微分聽覺迴路（Differentiable Auditory Loop, DAL），這是一個新的開源框架，用於個性化助聽器的設計和調整。我們的第一個DAL實現包含了CARFAC，這是一個可微分的人類耳蝸功能模型，我們將其移植到JAX，以優化深度神經網絡，使其能夠將受損的聽覺神經活動模式與正常聽力的參考進行匹配。為了構建一個具備細緻頻譜-時間信號處理能力的助聽器，我們採用了SEANet，一種波形到波形的全卷積UNet生成器。我們通過比較適合正常聽力的CARFAC模型的輸出與適合每位受試者個別聽力損失的CARFAC模型的輸出來微調網絡。比較是使用來自各自CARFAC神經活動模式（NAP）輸出和穩定聽覺影像（SAI）的損失函數進行的，後者提供了一種2D表示，捕捉了聽神經輸出中的相位不敏感時間結構。通過梯度下降，SEANet模型學會了去噪輸入並補償由受損的CARFAC模型所模擬的聽力損失。在神經表示和信號保真度指標中，經DAL優化的SEANet模型超越了測試的主助聽器（MHA）基準。DAL框架提供了一條實用的途徑，朝向基於模型的、機器學習驅動的助聽器信號處理個性化。接下來的步驟包括硬體部署，以便進行現實世界的臨床測試。

##### **From 'What' to 'How' and 'Why': Sharing LLM-Generated Retrospective Summaries of Older Adults' Passive Tracking Data with Remote Family Members**
2606.03876v1 by Jiachen Li, Reina Szeyi Chan, Akshat Choube, Xiang Zhi Tan, Elizabeth Mynatt, Varun Mishra

With the growing prevalence of modern ubiquitous computing technologies, multi-modal tracking systems hold promise for providing timely awareness and reassurance to stakeholders such as remote family members (RFMs) of older adults, who play a central role in care coordination. However, combining heterogeneous data streams into high-level, meaningful content - such as retrospective summaries - remains challenging. While recent work has demonstrated the promise of large language models (LLMs) for interpreting multi-modal tracking data, less attention has been given to generating narrative accounts for stakeholders like RFMs, who possess rich personal knowledge of older adults and strong emotional responsibility, yet have limited visibility into their daily lives and limited capacity for caregiving. In this work, we explore how LLMs can be used to generate retrospective summaries from multi-modal tracking data for RFMs of older adults. We leveraged and customized an existing system, Vital Insight, to generate initial summaries on different dates and data availability scenarios as technology probes, and conducted interviews with 11 RFMs to gather feedback. Based on these insights, we redesigned the system into a multi-layer, multi-agent, insight-driven summary approach that builds from objective statistics and descriptions to enriched, context-aware narratives. We then compared the redesigned summaries with the initial versions through a survey with the same 11 RFMs and found significant improvements in satisfaction, perceived helpfulness, trust, and willingness to receive the summaries. We conclude by presenting design implications for AI-generated summaries for RFMs and broader contexts, emphasizing the need to support RFMs' sensemaking shift from simply presenting ''What'' data were collected, to explaining ''How'' is my loved one doing and ''Why''.

摘要：隨著現代無處不在計算技術的日益普及，多模態追蹤系統有望為利益相關者提供及時的認知和安慰，例如老年人的遠程家庭成員（RFMs），他們在護理協調中扮演著核心角色。<lb/>然而，將異質數據流合併為高層次、有意義的內容——例如回顧性摘要——仍然具有挑戰性。<lb/>儘管最近的研究已展示大型語言模型（LLMs）在解釋多模態追蹤數據方面的潛力，但對於生成像RFMs這樣的利益相關者的敘述賬戶的關注較少，這些RFMs對老年人擁有豐富的個人知識和強烈的情感責任，但對他們的日常生活的可見性有限，且照顧能力有限。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們探討了如何利用LLMs為老年人的RFMs生成多模態追蹤數據的回顧性摘要。<lb/>我們利用並自定義了一個現有系統Vital Insight，以在不同日期和數據可用性場景下生成初步摘要，作為技術探針，並與11位RFMs進行了訪談以收集反饋。<lb/>根據這些見解，我們將系統重新設計為一種多層次、多代理的洞察驅動摘要方法，從客觀統計和描述構建到豐富的、具上下文意識的敘述。<lb/>然後，我們通過對同樣的11位RFMs進行調查，將重新設計的摘要與初始版本進行比較，發現滿意度、感知幫助性、信任度和接受摘要的意願均有顯著改善。<lb/>最後，我們提出了針對RFMs和更廣泛背景的AI生成摘要的設計啟示，強調支持RFMs從單純呈現「收集了什麼」數據，轉向解釋「我的摯愛過得怎麼樣」和「為什麼」的意義。

##### **Conditional Latent Diffusion Model with Fourier-based Motion Modelling for Virtual Population Synthesis**
2606.03827v1 by Shaokun Lan, Haoran Dou, Jinghan Huang, Arezoo Zakeri, Fengming Lin, Zherui Zhou, Jinming Duan, Alejandro F. Frangi

In-silico trials of medical devices require the generation of virtual populations of anatomies. In cardiovascular applications, virtual anatomy is typically represented as a 3D+t mesh sampled from a generative model. However, most existing mesh generators focus on static anatomy, while sequence models often lack explicit periodicity. To this end, we propose 4D F-MeshLDM, a conditional generative framework comprising a convolutional mesh VAE to encode meshes, a structural latent space that parameterises motion using a truncated Fourier series, and a diffusion prior that learns the latent distribution over Fourier coefficient tokens. By conditioning the diffusion process on clinical covariates via affine modulation, we enable controllable synthesis. Sampling tokens and performing inverse Fourier synthesis yield cycle-consistent latent trajectories, which can be decoded into 3D+t cardiac mesh sequences. Experiments on 5,000 UK Biobank subjects demonstrate that 4D F-MeshLDM outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in anatomical fidelity and achieves near-zero cycle closure error. Furthermore, the generated cohorts accurately preserve clinical functional indices, highlighting the potential of our framework for reliable in-silico cardiac trials.

##### **Need to Know: Contextual-Integrity-Grounded Query Rewriting for Privacy-Conscious LLM Delegation**
2606.04067v1 by Xinyue Huang, Xiaochun Cao, Wenyuan Yang

As LLMs become increasingly woven into everyday workflows, user queries sent to cloud hosted LLMs routinely mix task-essential content with task non-essential sensitive disclosures, yet type based PII redaction is context agnostic and may raise two issues: over disclosing untyped sensitive context and over removing answer bearing spans. We recast privacy preserving query rewriting under Contextual Integrity: a span should be forwarded only if it is necessary for the task. We introduce DelegateCI-Bench, the first task based Contextual Integrity benchmark for privacy-conscious delegation, comprising 3,167 samples that combine high quality synthetic data spanning 11 tasks and 20 task types, WildChat based real user queries, and a medical challenge set with dense sensitive information. Building on this benchmark, we propose a CI-guided reinforcement learning framework that converts essential and non-essential sensitive spans into verifiable optimization signals, and train a query rewriter to preserve task critical information while suppressing unnecessary sensitive disclosure. Experiments show that our learned rewriter achieves the best privacy-utility tradeoff, achieving up to +10.1 average utility over on-device baselines.

摘要：隨著大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地融入日常工作流程，發送到雲端託管的LLMs的用戶查詢通常將任務必需的內容與任務非必需的敏感披露混合在一起，但基於類型的個人身份信息（PII）刪除是與上下文無關的，可能會引發兩個問題：過度披露未標記的敏感上下文和過度刪除包含答案的範圍。我們在上下文完整性下重新構建了隱私保護的查詢重寫：只有在對任務必要時，範圍才應被轉發。我們介紹了DelegateCI-Bench，這是首個基於任務的上下文完整性基準，用於注重隱私的委派，包含3,167個樣本，結合了涵蓋11個任務和20個任務類型的高質量合成數據、基於WildChat的真實用戶查詢，以及一個包含密集敏感信息的醫療挑戰集。在這個基準的基礎上，我們提出了一個CI引導的強化學習框架，將必需和非必需的敏感範圍轉換為可驗證的優化信號，並訓練一個查詢重寫器以保留任務關鍵信息，同時抑制不必要的敏感披露。實驗表明，我們學習的重寫器實現了最佳的隱私-效用權衡，平均效用比設備基準高出10.1%。

##### **Gender-Dependent Diagnostic Substitution in LLM Medical Triage: Same Symptoms, Unequal Urgency**
2606.03641v1 by Qi Han Wong

We investigate whether large language models produce different medical triage recommendations for identical neurological symptoms when only the patient's stated gender and age vary. Using three model families--Gemini 3.5 Flash, Claude Sonnet 4.6, and GPT-5.4-mini--we present a standardized symptom profile (persistent headache, blurred vision, morning nausea, visual disturbances) across seven demographic conditions: three age groups (25, 38, 65) x two genders (male, female), plus a gender-unspecified baseline (n = 30 per condition per model, 630 total trials). We find a stark, systemic gender-dependent triage disparity: young women receive significantly lower emergency room (ER) referral rates than age-matched men (Gemini: 0% vs. 23.3%; Claude: 6.7% vs. 96.7%; GPT: 6.7% vs. 66.7%, all p < 0.001). The disparity disappears at age 65 for all models. The primary mechanism is diagnostic substitution: the models anchor on a gender-associated diagnosis, preferentially classifying young women with Idiopathic Intracranial Hypertension (IIH)--a condition epidemiologically linked to women of childbearing age--while diagnosing men with generic increased intracranial pressure with space-occupying lesions in the differential. This diagnostic closure routes female patients to lower-urgency care (outpatient doctor appointments) despite comparable severity ratings (7-9/10). Our findings demonstrate that clinical LLMs replicate documented human clinical biases by using epidemiological priors to suppress triage urgency, suggesting that AI triage engines must decouple urgency assessment from probabilistic diagnostic priors. We release all code, prompts, and raw results.

摘要：我們調查大型語言模型是否會對相同的神經症狀產生不同的醫療分診建議，當僅有病人的性別和年齡變化時。使用三個模型系列——Gemini 3.5 Flash、Claude Sonnet 4.6 和 GPT-5.4-mini——我們在七個人口統計條件下呈現一個標準化的症狀檔案（持續性頭痛、視力模糊、早晨噁心、視覺干擾）：三個年齡組（25、38、65歲）x 兩個性別（男性、女性），加上一個性別未指定的基線（每個條件每個模型 n = 30，共630次試驗）。我們發現明顯的系統性性別依賴性分診差異：年輕女性的急診室（ER）轉診率顯著低於年齡相符的男性（Gemini: 0% vs. 23.3%；Claude: 6.7% vs. 96.7%；GPT: 6.7% vs. 66.7%，均 p < 0.001）。對於所有模型，這種差異在65歲時消失。主要機制是診斷替代：模型基於性別相關的診斷，優先將年輕女性歸類為特發性顱內高壓（IIH）——這是一種流行病學上與育齡女性相關的病症——而將男性診斷為具有占位性病變的普通顱內壓增高。這種診斷封閉將女性患者引導至低緊急性護理（門診醫生預約），儘管嚴重程度評分相當（7-9/10）。我們的研究結果顯示，臨床大型語言模型通過使用流行病學先驗來抑制分診緊急性，複製了已記錄的人類臨床偏見，這表明 AI 分診引擎必須將緊急性評估與概率診斷先驗解耦。我們釋放所有代碼、提示和原始結果。

##### **VidMsg: A Benchmark for Implicit Message Inference in Short Videos**
2606.03635v1 by Issar Tzachor, Michael Green, Rami Ben-Ari

Understanding short online videos involves more than identifying visible objects and actions; video makers often include an underlying message or purpose in the clip. We introduce VidMsg, a benchmark for evaluating implicit message understanding in short, internet-native video clips. VidMsg contains 400 YouTube-derived clips across 9 practical topic areas and 52 fine-grained target messages, covering domains such as career and finance, education, health and well-being, culture, safety, sustainability, and lifestyle. VidMsg is constructed through a message-first pipeline: an LLM first translates target messages into indirect search scenarios, which are used to retrieve candidate clips. Human annotators then retain clips that convey the intended message without being overly explicit. VidMsg is designed primarily for bidirectional message-clip retrieval for scalable applications such as video search and recommendation, where systems must capture holistic video understanding. In addition to retrieval, VidMsg includes a diagnostic multiple-choice QA benchmark, where models select the intended message of a clip from semantically related alternatives. Experiments with contemporary video-language and retrieval models show that strong models often fail on VidMsg, because the task requires pragmatic inference, integration of contextual cues, and discrimination among semantically close messages. We also introduce VidVec-Msg, a baseline method that improves message-oriented retrieval while leaving substantial headroom for future work.

摘要：了解短小的在線視頻不僅僅是識別可見的物體和行為；視頻製作者通常會在片段中包含潛在的訊息或目的。<lb/>我們介紹了VidMsg，這是一個用於評估短小、網絡原生視頻片段中隱含訊息理解的基準。<lb/>VidMsg包含來自YouTube的400個片段，涵蓋9個實用主題領域和52個細緻的目標訊息，涉及職業和財務、教育、健康與福祉、文化、安全、可持續性和生活方式等領域。<lb/>VidMsg是通過一個以訊息為先的流程構建的：一個大型語言模型首先將目標訊息轉換為間接搜索場景，這些場景用於檢索候選片段。<lb/>然後，人類標註者保留那些傳達預期訊息但不過於明確的片段。<lb/>VidMsg主要設計用於雙向訊息-片段檢索，以支持可擴展的應用，如視頻搜索和推薦，這些系統必須捕捉整體視頻理解。<lb/>除了檢索，VidMsg還包括一個診斷性的多選題問答基準，模型需從語義相關的選項中選擇片段的預期訊息。<lb/>與當代視頻-語言和檢索模型的實驗顯示，強大的模型在VidMsg上經常失敗，因為這項任務需要實用推理、上下文線索的整合以及在語義相近的訊息之間的區分。<lb/>我們還介紹了VidVec-Msg，一種基準方法，改善了以訊息為導向的檢索，同時為未來的工作留出了相當的發展空間。

##### **AnchorMoE: Interpretable Time Series Classification via Anchor-Routed MoE**
2606.03631v2 by Tao Xie, Zexi Tan, Haoyi Xiao, Mengke Li, Yiqun Zhang, Yang Lu, Cuie Yang, Yiu-ming Cheung

Multivariate time series classification (MTSC) is pivotal in high-stakes domains, such as clinical diagnosis and industrial fault detection, where safe deployment necessitates transparent decision-making. However, isolating the temporal segments that drive model predictions is challenging because discriminative signals in real-world time series are typically sparse, heterogeneous, and heavily obscured by background noise. This paper, therefore, proposes AnchorMoE, an interpretable-by-construction classification framework. Built upon a Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architecture, AnchorMoE encodes multi-view representations of local patches and routes them to specialized experts, ensuring that the final prediction is formulated as an exact additive decomposition over the input segments, facilitating ante-hoc transparency rather than relying on post-hoc estimations. To maintain the reliability of this decomposition under sparse signal distributions, we introduce a geometric orthogonality constraint that penalizes representational redundancy, compelling distinct experts to specialize in heterogeneous predictive patterns. Furthermore, an uncertainty-aware reliability gate is designed to dynamically calibrate the contribution of each segment, effectively suppressing residual background noise. Extensive experiments on real-world and synthetic benchmarks demonstrate that AnchorMoE achieves highly competitive classification performance while faithfully grounding its decisions in the raw time series.

摘要：多變量時間序列分類 (MTSC) 在高風險領域中至關重要，例如臨床診斷和工業故障檢測，這些領域的安全部署需要透明的決策過程。<lb/>然而，隔離驅動模型預測的時間段是具有挑戰性的，因為現實世界時間序列中的區分信號通常稀疏、異質，並且受到背景噪音的嚴重掩蓋。<lb/>因此，本文提出了 AnchorMoE，一個可解釋的分類框架。<lb/>AnchorMoE 基於專家混合 (MoE) 架構，編碼局部區塊的多視角表示，並將其路由到專門的專家，確保最終預測作為輸入段的精確加法分解來形成，促進事前透明性，而不是依賴事後估計。<lb/>為了在稀疏信號分佈下保持這種分解的可靠性，我們引入了一個幾何正交性約束，對表示冗餘進行懲罰，迫使不同的專家專注於異質的預測模式。<lb/>此外，設計了一個考慮不確定性的可靠性閘，以動態校準每個段的貢獻，有效抑制殘留的背景噪音。<lb/>在現實世界和合成基準上的廣泛實驗表明，AnchorMoE 在分類性能上達到了高度競爭的水平，同時忠實地將其決策根植於原始時間序列中。

##### **Efficient Transformer-Based Localized Patch Sampling for Choroid Plexus Segmentation in Multiple Sclerosis**
2606.03566v1 by Po-Jui Lu, Alessandro Cagol, Mario Ocampo-Pineda, Federico Spagnolo, Marina Mastantuono, Andreea-Alexandra Aldea, Jannis Müller, Özgür Yaldizli, Matthias Weigel, Lester Melie-Garcia, Roberta Magliozzi, Maria Pia Sormani, Ludwig Kappos, Jens Kuhle, Cristina Granziera

##### **Scalable On-Hardware Training of Quantum Neural Networks and Application to Clinical Data Imputation**
2606.03517v1 by Natansh Mathur, Panagiotis Kl. Barkoutsos, Masako Yamada, Martin Roetteler, Iordanis Kerenidis

Training quantum neural networks (QNNs) on quantum hardware is currently bottlenecked by the cost of gradient estimation: standard parameter-shift methods require a number of circuit evaluations that grows quadratically with the number of trainable parameters, making hardware-based optimisation impractical beyond small system sizes. In this work, we introduce a training framework that reduces this cost to logarithmic in the number of qubits, making gradient-based QNN optimisation feasible on near-term hardware at increasing scales.
  Our framework combines three co-designed ingredients: (i) a structured, subspace-preserving Butterfly circuit architecture with $O(n \log n)$ parameters and logarithmic depth; (ii) a layer-wise training strategy that confines on-hardware optimisation to one small, well-structured layer at a time; and (iii) a parallelised parameter-shift rule that exploits the commuting structure within each Butterfly layer to extract all gradients in a constant number of circuit executions. Together these reduce the number of distinct circuit evaluations per optimisation step from $O(n^2)$ to $O(\log n)$.
  We validate the framework on clinical data imputation using the MIMIC-III electronic health record dataset, a demanding benchmark sensitive to optimisation instability and model variance. Hybrid classical-quantum models are trained directly on IonQ Forte Enterprise trapped-ion hardware at 16 qubits without performance degradation relative to ideal or noisy simulation and via tensor-network simulation at 32 qubits, with 32-qubit inference executed on hardware. The resulting models match or exceed strong classical neural baselines in downstream patient survival prediction while exhibiting reduced variance across runs, demonstrating that the proposed framework enables practical, scalable QNN training under realistic hardware constraints.

摘要：訓練量子神經網絡（QNNs）在量子硬體上的過程目前受到梯度估計成本的瓶頸：標準的參數轉移方法需要的電路評估次數隨著可訓練參數的數量呈平方增長，這使得基於硬體的優化在超過小型系統時變得不切實際。在本研究中，我們介紹了一種訓練框架，將這一成本降低到與量子位數量呈對數關係，使得基於梯度的QNN優化在近期硬體上在不斷增大的規模上變得可行。<lb/>
我們的框架結合了三個共同設計的要素：（i）一種結構化的、保持子空間的蝴蝶電路架構，具有$O(n \log n)$的參數和對數深度；（ii）一種分層訓練策略，將在硬體上的優化限制在一個小而結構良好的層次上；以及（iii）一種並行化的參數轉移規則，利用每個蝴蝶層內的可交換結構，在恆定數量的電路執行中提取所有梯度。這些共同將每次優化步驟所需的不同電路評估次數從$O(n^2)$減少到$O(\log n)$。<lb/>
我們在臨床數據插補上驗證了該框架，使用MIMIC-III電子健康記錄數據集，這是一個對優化不穩定性和模型變異性敏感的挑戰性基準。混合經典-量子模型直接在16量子位的IonQ Forte Enterprise捕獲離子硬體上訓練，與理想或噪聲模擬相比沒有性能下降，並通過32量子位的張量網絡模擬進行，32量子位的推斷在硬體上執行。所得到的模型在下游患者生存預測中匹配或超過強大的經典神經基準，同時在多次運行中顯示出減少的變異性，證明了所提出的框架能夠在現實的硬體限制下實現實用的、可擴展的QNN訓練。

##### **Multi-Modal Graph Neural Network with Transformer-Guided Adaptive Diffusion for Preclinical Alzheimer Classification**
2606.03322v1 by Jaeyoon Sim, Minjae Lee, Guorong Wu, Won Hwa Kim

The graphical representation of the brain offers critical insights into diagnosing and prognosing neurodegenerative disease via relationships between regions of interest (ROIs). Despite recent emergence of various Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) to effectively capture the relational information, there remain inherent limitations in interpreting the brain networks. Specifically, convolutional approaches ineffectively aggregate information from distant neighborhoods, while attention-based methods exhibit deficiencies in capturing node-centric information, particularly in retaining critical characteristics from pivotal nodes. These shortcomings reveal challenges for identifying disease-specific variation from diverse features from different modalities. In this regard, we propose an integrated framework guiding diffusion process at each node by a downstream transformer where both short- and long-range properties of graphs are aggregated via diffusion-kernel and multi-head attention respectively. We demonstrate the superiority of our model by improving performance of pre-clinical Alzheimer's disease (AD) classification with various modalities. Also, our model adeptly identifies key ROIs that are closely associated with the preclinical stages of AD, marking a significant potential for early diagnosis and prevision of the disease.

摘要：腦部的圖形表示提供了關鍵的見解，用於通過感興趣區域 (ROIs) 之間的關係來診斷和預測神經退行性疾病。儘管最近出現了各種圖神經網絡 (GNNs) 以有效捕捉關係信息，但在解釋腦網絡方面仍然存在固有的限制。具體而言，卷積方法無法有效地聚合來自遙遠鄰域的信息，而基於注意力的方法在捕捉以節點為中心的信息方面存在不足，特別是在保留關鍵節點的關鍵特徵方面。這些缺陷揭示了從不同模態的多樣特徵中識別疾病特定變異的挑戰。在這方面，我們提出了一個綜合框架，通過下游Transformer引導每個節點的擴散過程，其中圖的短距離和長距離特性分別通過擴散核和多頭注意力進行聚合。我們通過提高各種模態的臨床前阿茲海默病 (AD) 分類性能來展示我們模型的優越性。此外，我們的模型熟練地識別與AD臨床前階段密切相關的關鍵ROIs，標誌著早期診斷和預測該疾病的重大潛力。

##### **The Reliability Gap in Benchmark Auditing: Distribution Shift and Scale as Failure Modes of Contamination Detection**
2606.03305v1 by Wojciech Zarzecki, Jan Dubiński, Sebastian Cygert

Benchmark contamination, where evaluation examples appear in a model's training data, threatens the validity of LLM assessment. Statistical tools for detecting training-data membership exist, but have been validated almost exclusively in controlled academic regimes: large, homogeneous pre-training corpora and transparent, single-stage training pipelines. Whether these methods remain reliable in realistic auditing scenarios remains unclear. We identify two under-studied failure modes: distribution shift, which arises when suspect and validation sets violate the IID assumption, and scale constraints, which arise because benchmarks are orders of magnitude smaller than pre-training corpora. We systematically evaluate three leading paradigms: LLM Dataset Inference, Post-Hoc Dataset Inference, and CoDeC across 27 models from multiple families (including Pythia, OLMo~2, and specialised cultural and medical LLMs) and scales (up to 27B). We then further extend our analysis to frontier industry models. Across 335 evaluations, only 199 yield correct outcomes. LLM Dataset Inference results in false positives under distribution shift, Post-Hoc Dataset Inference is underpowered at benchmark scale, and CoDeC provides only coarse provenance signals that are insufficient to verify individual benchmark splits. Our results reveal a systematic reliability gap between controlled validation and practical benchmark auditing, and show that statistical detection cannot yet replace transparent data provenance. We open-source our benchmark for further research.

摘要：基準污染，即評估範例出現在模型的訓練數據中，威脅著LLM評估的有效性。雖然存在檢測訓練數據成員資格的統計工具，但這些工具幾乎僅在受控的學術環境中得到驗證：大型、同質的預訓練語料庫和透明的單階段訓練流程。這些方法在現實審計場景中是否仍然可靠尚不清楚。我們確定了兩種未充分研究的失效模式：分佈轉移，當可疑集和驗證集違反IID假設時產生，以及規模限制，因為基準的規模比預訓練語料庫小幾個數量級。我們系統地評估了三種主要範式：LLM數據集推理、事後數據集推理和CoDeC，涵蓋來自多個家族（包括Pythia、OLMo~2，以及專門的文化和醫療LLM）和規模（高達27B）的27個模型。然後，我們進一步將分析擴展到前沿行業模型。在335次評估中，僅有199次產生正確的結果。LLM數據集推理在分佈轉移下導致假陽性，事後數據集推理在基準規模下能力不足，而CoDeC僅提供粗略的來源信號，無法驗證單個基準拆分。我們的結果揭示了受控驗證與實際基準審計之間的系統可靠性差距，並表明統計檢測尚無法取代透明的數據來源。我們將基準開源以供進一步研究。

##### **MedCUA-Bench: A Screenshot-Only Benchmark for Clinical Computer-Use Agents**
2606.03203v1 by Jia Yu, Zilong Wang, Xinyang Jiang, Dongsheng Li, Shuo Wang

Computer-use agents could automate repetitive screen-based clinical work, but their reliability in medical graphical user interfaces remains largely unvalidated. Existing benchmarks focus on general web or desktop tasks and underrepresent medical software, which requires domain knowledge, exhibits markedly different UI design from mainstream applications, lacks public testing environments, and demands safety validation beyond task completion. We introduce MedCUA-Bench, an interactive benchmark for clinical computer-use agents. It covers 18 clinical scenarios across 10 medical domains, reconstructed from real product manuals and open-source medical systems to capture authentic clinical interfaces while avoiding licensing and privacy constraints. Each task ships with paired intent- and step-level goals to disentangle clinical reasoning from UI execution, and is evaluated by a deterministic checker over task completion and five clinical safety dimensions. Across 23 agents, the best closed-source model reaches 54.2% strict success, while all models remain below 9% on the real OpenEMR. Open-source agents average only 2.5%, with the best reaching 16.2%. MedCUA-Bench exposes the gap between current agents and reliable clinical software use, providing a reproducible testbed for future research.

摘要：電腦使用代理可以自動化重複的基於螢幕的臨床工作，但它們在醫療圖形用戶界面中的可靠性仍然在很大程度上未經驗證。現有的基準測試專注於一般的網頁或桌面任務，並且對醫療軟體的代表性不足，因為醫療軟體需要專業知識，展現出與主流應用截然不同的用戶界面設計，缺乏公共測試環境，並且要求超越任務完成的安全驗證。我們介紹了 MedCUA-Bench，一個針對臨床電腦使用代理的互動基準測試。它涵蓋了 10 個醫療領域中的 18 個臨床場景，這些場景是從真實產品手冊和開源醫療系統重建而來，以捕捉真實的臨床界面，同時避免授權和隱私限制。每個任務都附有配對的意圖和步驟級目標，以解開臨床推理與用戶界面執行之間的關聯，並由確定性檢查器在任務完成和五個臨床安全維度上進行評估。在 23 個代理中，最佳的閉源模型達到 54.2% 的嚴格成功率，而所有模型在真實的 OpenEMR 上均低於 9%。開源代理的平均成功率僅為 2.5%，最佳的達到 16.2%。MedCUA-Bench 揭示了當前代理與可靠臨床軟體使用之間的差距，為未來的研究提供了一個可重複的測試平台。

##### **AI Rater Discrimination Depends on Scoring Protocol in Complex Clinical Decision-Making**
2606.03198v1 by Sangwon Baek, Kyu Yeon Hur, Kyunga Kim

Clinical AI evaluation increasingly delegates scoring to large language models (LLMs) acting as AI raters, yet their scoring behavior across evaluation conditions has not been quantitatively characterized. We address this gap through a factorial study of AI rater behavior in adult type 2 diabetes (T2D) pharmacotherapy at 12-month outpatient follow-up, a clinical task involving complex decision-making operationalized across seven evaluation questions. Four open-source LLMs served simultaneously as clinical decision support system (CDSS) models and AI raters. Each CDSS output was scored under two scoring protocols: a rubric-anchored Gold Rubric (GR) protocol incorporating a patient-specific rubric, and a rubric-free Non Gold Rubric (Non-GR) protocol. Linear mixed effects models crossed the scoring protocol factor with five design factors -- CDSS model, CDSS prompt configuration (document-referenced generation [DRG] vs.\ Baseline), rater model, prompt character, and prompt type -- and estimated main effects together with their protocol interactions. Across all questions, AI raters yielded consistently higher scores within a very narrow range (74--78 points on average) under Non-GR compared to those under GR (7.69 to 49.64 points lower mean scores; 1.68 to 3.67 times wider interquartile ranges). Within each question, GR amplified the AI rater's discrimination between DRG and Baseline CDSS outputs by factors of 1.76 to 5.10, while also revealing substantial behavioral variation across rater models that Non-GR suppressed. These findings support rubric anchoring as the scoring protocol that preserves discriminative power in clinical AI evaluation; rubric-free scoring cannot substitute when questions require patient-specific or jurisdiction-specific criteria that rater models cannot infer from parametric knowledge alone.

摘要：臨床 AI 評估越來越多地將評分委託給作為 AI 評分員的大型語言模型 (LLMs)，然而它們在不同評估條件下的評分行為尚未被定量特徵化。<lb/>我們通過對成人 2 型糖尿病 (T2D) 藥物治療在 12 個月門診隨訪中的 AI 評分員行為進行的因子研究來填補這一空白，這是一項涉及複雜決策的臨床任務，涵蓋七個評估問題。<lb/>四個開源 LLM 同時作為臨床決策支持系統 (CDSS) 模型和 AI 評分員。<lb/>每個 CDSS 輸出在兩個評分協議下進行評分：一個以評分標準為基礎的金標準 (GR) 協議，包含患者特定的評分標準，以及一個無評分標準的非金標準 (Non-GR) 協議。<lb/>線性混合效應模型將評分協議因素與五個設計因素交叉——CDSS 模型、CDSS 提示配置（文件參考生成 [DRG] 與基線）、評分員模型、提示字符和提示類型——並估計主要效應及其協議交互作用。<lb/>在所有問題中，AI 評分員在 Non-GR 下的評分始終高於 GR，且範圍非常狹窄（平均 74 至 78 分），與 GR 下的評分相比，平均分數低 7.69 至 49.64 分；四分位數範圍擴大 1.68 至 3.67 倍。<lb/>在每個問題中，GR 增強了 AI 評分員對 DRG 和基線 CDSS 輸出的區分能力，增幅為 1.76 至 5.10，同時揭示了不同評分員模型之間的顯著行為變異，而 Non-GR 則抑制了這種變異。<lb/>這些發現支持以評分標準為基礎的評分協議，該協議在臨床 AI 評估中保留了區分能力；當問題需要患者特定或管轄特定標準，而評分員模型無法僅通過參數知識推斷時，無評分標準的評分無法替代。

#### Abstracts
##### **A Unifying Lens on Supervised Fine-Tuning Through Target Distribution Design**
2606.11189v1 by Tong Xie, Yuanhao Ban, Yunqi Hong, Sohyun An, Yihang Chen, Cho-Jui Hsieh

Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) typically maximizes the likelihood of every token in a demonstrated trajectory. However, an observed token can be non-unique, noisy, or misaligned with the model prior. Strictly fitting toward this one-hot target may be suboptimal, especially when the pretrained model encodes a rich knowledge prior. In this work, we reinterpret SFT as target distribution design: instead of studying only the loss objective, we analyze the token-level target that the loss drives the model to match. We introduce the Q-target framework, which decomposes SFT supervision into two explicit choices: (1) how strongly to rely on the observed token, and (2) how to allocate the remaining probability mass over alternatives. This perspective unifies many existing SFT variants as implicit choices of the target distribution Q. Building on this view, we propose Target-SFT which constructs the training objective directly from the desired target distribution. This method consistently outperforms across the ten reasoning dataset-model settings evaluated, showing the effectiveness of this target-based approach. Overall, our formulation reveals a more fundamental design principle for SFT training and opens a broader search space for SFT objectives.

摘要：監督微調 (SFT) 通常會最大化每個在示範軌跡中的標記的可能性。<lb/>然而，觀察到的標記可能是非唯一的、嘈雜的，或與模型的先驗不一致。<lb/>嚴格地朝著這個單一目標進行擬合可能不是最佳的，特別是當預訓練模型編碼了豐富的知識先驗時。<lb/>在本研究中，我們將 SFT 重新詮釋為目標分佈設計：我們不僅研究損失目標，還分析損失驅動模型匹配的標記級目標。<lb/>我們引入了 Q-target 框架，將 SFT 監督分解為兩個明確的選擇：(1) 依賴觀察到的標記的強度，和 (2) 如何將剩餘的概率質量分配給其他選擇。<lb/>這種觀點統一了許多現有的 SFT 變體，作為目標分佈 Q 的隱含選擇。<lb/>基於這一觀點，我們提出了 Target-SFT，該方法直接從所需的目標分佈構建訓練目標。<lb/>這種方法在評估的十個推理數據集-模型設置中始終表現優於其他方法，顯示了這種基於目標的方法的有效性。<lb/>總體而言，我們的公式揭示了 SFT 訓練的一個更基本的設計原則，並為 SFT 目標開辟了更廣泛的搜索空間。

##### **Flaws in the LLM Automation Narrative**
2606.11166v1 by George Perrett, Javae Elliott, Jennifer Hill, Marc Scott

Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly described as performing at the level of human experts on knowledge economy tasks. These claims are primarily based on how LLMs perform on benchmarking tasks that measure average performance across standardized datasets. Primary limitations of many benchmarking tasks are that they often measure performance based on content directly included in LLM training data, and they frequently do not assess the reliability of LLM performance or the magnitude of LLM errors. However, in high stakes contexts, these qualities are critically important. Through a novel LLM benchmarking task that requires writing computer code to complete a data analysis task, we compare the performance of a frontier LLM against submissions from human experts and explicitly measure the variance of responses and the magnitude of errors. Our study reveals that the human experts perform better on average on a range of metrics and demonstrate less variability in performance. Our results provide evidence that LLMs do not consistently perform at the level of human experts and demonstrate the importance of measuring variance and assessing error magnitude in LLM benchmark evaluations.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地被描述為在知識經濟任務中達到人類專家的水平。這些說法主要基於LLMs在基準任務中的表現，這些任務測量的是在標準化數據集上的平均表現。許多基準任務的主要限制在於，它們通常根據直接包含在LLM訓練數據中的內容來衡量表現，並且經常不評估LLM表現的可靠性或LLM錯誤的大小。然而，在高風險的情境中，這些特質是至關重要的。通過一項新穎的LLM基準任務，要求編寫計算機代碼以完成數據分析任務，我們將前沿LLM的表現與人類專家的提交進行比較，並明確測量反應的變異性和錯誤的大小。我們的研究顯示，人類專家在多個指標上的平均表現更佳，並且表現的變異性較小。我們的結果提供了證據表明LLMs並不總是能夠達到人類專家的水平，並且顯示了在LLM基準評估中測量變異性和評估錯誤大小的重要性。

##### **ABC-Bench: An Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark for Biosecurity**
2606.11150v1 by Andrew Bo Liu, Samira Nedungadi, Bryce Cai, Alex Kleinman, Harmon Bhasin, Seth Donoughe

Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly acquiring capabilities relevant to biological research, from literature synthesis to interpretation of experimental data. Increasingly, LLM agents can also perform in silico biology tasks that previously required experienced human biologists. These emerging AI capabilities offer new opportunities for scientific discovery and biomedical advances, but they also shift the landscape of biosecurity risks. To address this, we introduce the Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark (ABC-Bench), a suite of tasks to measure agentic biosecurity-relevant capabilities. ABC-Bench evaluates LLM agents on both benign and dual-use biology tasks: writing code to operate liquid handling robots, designing DNA fragments for in vitro assembly, and evading DNA synthesis screening. These tasks require a combination of biology and software expertise. All tested LLM agents outperformed the median expert human baseliner on all three tasks. Agents performed highly on tasks drawing on published knowledge and well-documented protocols, and more weakly on a task requiring novel bioinformatics reasoning. In three wet-lab validation experiments, we found that OpenAI's o4-mini-high produced scripts that, when run on an OpenTrons liquid handling robot, successfully assembled DNA with expected sequences.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）正在迅速獲得與生物研究相關的能力，從文獻綜述到實驗數據的解釋。越來越多的 LLM 代理也能執行以前需要經驗豐富的人類生物學家的計算生物學任務。這些新興的 AI 能力為科學發現和生物醫學進步提供了新的機會，但它們也改變了生物安全風險的格局。為了解決這個問題，我們介紹了代理生物能力基準（ABC-Bench），這是一套用於測量與生物安全相關的代理能力的任務。ABC-Bench 在良性和雙用途生物學任務上評估 LLM 代理：編寫操作液體處理機器人的代碼、設計用於體外組裝的 DNA 片段，以及躲避 DNA 合成篩查。這些任務需要生物學和軟件專業知識的結合。所有測試的 LLM 代理在這三項任務上均超過了中位數專家人類基準。代理在依賴已發表知識和良好記錄的協議的任務上表現優異，而在需要新穎生物信息學推理的任務上表現較弱。在三個濕實驗室驗證實驗中，我們發現 OpenAI 的 o4-mini-high 生成的腳本在 OpenTrons 液體處理機器人上運行時，成功組裝了具有預期序列的 DNA。

##### **Towards Autonomous Accelerator Design: FPGA Accelerator Generation with SECDA**
2606.11117v1 by Vinamra Sharma, Xingjian Fu, Jude Haris, José Cano

Designing FPGA-based accelerators for modern artificial intelligence workloads requires exploring a large and complex hardware design space that involves architectural parameters, data flow strategies, and memory hierarchies, making the process very time consuming. While existing methodologies such as SECDA enable rapid hardware-software co-design through SystemC simulation and FPGA execution, identifying efficient accelerator configurations remains a largely manual process requiring extensive domain knowledge. SECDA-DSE is a framework that integrates Large Language Models (LLMs) into the SECDA ecosystem to guide design space exploration (DSE) of FPGA-based accelerators. It combines a structured DSE Explorer for generating candidate architectures with an LLM Stack that performs reasoning-guided exploration using retrieval-augmented generation and chain-of-thought prompting, coupled with a feedback loop for iterative and reinforced refinement. Building on our previous work introducing SECDA-DSE, this paper extends its evaluation by generating three accelerator designs, including element-wise vector multiplication, 2D convolution, and matrix transpose, and performing end-to-end execution on FPGA hardware. The results show that SECDA-DSE can generate SECDA-compliant accelerator designs that are successfully synthesized and executed on FPGA hardware. Furthermore, the generated designs capture kernel-specific trade-offs between compute parallelism and data movement, highlighting the potential of LLM-guided exploration to adapt architectural configurations across diverse workloads while reducing exploration time and the need for extensive human expertise.

摘要：設計基於FPGA的加速器以應對現代人工智慧工作負載需要探索一個龐大且複雜的硬體設計空間，這涉及架構參數、數據流策略和記憶體層次，使得這個過程非常耗時。雖然現有的方法論如SECDA通過SystemC模擬和FPGA執行實現了快速的硬體-軟體共同設計，但識別高效的加速器配置仍然是一個主要依賴手動過程，需要廣泛的領域知識。SECDA-DSE是一個將大型語言模型（LLMs）整合進SECDA生態系統的框架，以指導基於FPGA的加速器的設計空間探索（DSE）。它結合了一個結構化的DSE探索器，用於生成候選架構，以及一個LLM堆疊，該堆疊使用檢索增強生成和思維鏈提示進行推理引導的探索，並配合一個反饋循環以進行迭代和強化的精煉。在我們之前的工作中介紹SECDA-DSE的基礎上，本文通過生成三個加速器設計，包括元素級向量乘法、2D卷積和矩陣轉置，並在FPGA硬體上進行端到端執行，擴展了其評估。結果顯示SECDA-DSE可以生成符合SECDA標準的加速器設計，這些設計成功地在FPGA硬體上進行合成和執行。此外，生成的設計捕捉了計算並行性和數據移動之間的內核特定權衡，突顯了LLM引導探索在適應多樣工作負載的架構配置方面的潛力，同時減少探索時間和對廣泛人類專業知識的需求。

##### **FADA: Accessible fetal ultrasound interpretation and annotation with a selectively distilled unified vision-language model**
2606.11106v1 by Mahmood Alzubaidi, Uzair Shah, Raden Muaz, Ines Abbes, Nader Mohammed, Abdullatif Magram, Khalid Alyafei, Mowafa Househ, Marco Agus

A global shortage of trained sonographers limits prenatal ultrasound screening in low- and middle-income countries, where over half of pregnant women receive no skilled sonography. Current deep learning approaches address detection, segmentation, or classification in isolation, each demanding a separate model and expert-specified labels at inference. We present FADA, a unified vision-language model built on Qwen3.5-VL that performs clinical interpretation, classification, detection, and segmentation through a single interpretation-first pipeline without external labels. FADA distills knowledge from four domain-specific foundation models (FetalCLIP, UltraSAM, USF-MAE, UltraFedFM) via offline pre-computed feature caching. Selective distillation, which applies feature alignment only to annotation tasks while interpretation relies on standard fine-tuning, consistently outperforms full distillation across most evaluation axes. The recommended variant, FADA-SKD, achieves 0.8820 mean Dice for segmentation, 0.7671 mAP@0.50 for detection, and 100% structured interpretation compliance. Expert sonographer validation across 237 images confirms clinically acceptable outputs in both autonomous and human-in-the-loop modes, with 73.5% of interpretations scoring perfectly under clinician guidance. The system is trainable on a single consumer GPU and deployable without cloud connectivity. We validate edge deployment by running the compressed 0.8B model on a commodity smartphone (Qualcomm Snapdragon 7 Gen 1, 12 GB RAM) using llama.cpp with GGUF quantization, completing the full 5-phase pipeline in approximately 60 seconds entirely offline. This establishes a practical pathway for integrating AI-assisted fetal assessment with portable ultrasound devices, directly addressing diagnostic access gaps in resource-constrained settings. Code, models, and data are available at https://github.com/mahmoodphd/FADA.

摘要：全球訓練有素的超聲醫生短缺限制了低收入和中等收入國家的產前超聲篩查，這些國家中有超過一半的孕婦沒有接受專業超聲檢查。當前的深度學習方法分別處理檢測、分割或分類，每個方法都需要一個單獨的模型和專家指定的標籤進行推斷。我們提出了FADA，一個基於Qwen3.5-VL的統一視覺-語言模型，通過單一的解釋優先管道執行臨床解釋、分類、檢測和分割，而不需要外部標籤。FADA通過離線預計算特徵緩存從四個特定領域的基礎模型（FetalCLIP、UltraSAM、USF-MAE、UltraFedFM）提煉知識。選擇性蒸餾僅將特徵對齊應用於標註任務，而解釋則依賴於標準微調，這在大多數評估指標上始終優於完全蒸餾。推薦變體FADA-SKD在分割中達到0.8820的平均Dice，在檢測中達到0.7671的mAP@0.50，以及100%的結構化解釋合規性。對237張圖像的專家超聲醫生驗證確認了在自主和人類參與模式下的臨床可接受輸出，其中73.5%的解釋在臨床醫生指導下得分完美。該系統可以在單個消費者GPU上進行訓練，並且可在沒有雲連接的情況下部署。我們通過在一部普通智能手機（高通Snapdragon 7 Gen 1，12 GB RAM）上運行壓縮的0.8B模型來驗證邊緣部署，使用llama.cpp進行GGUF量化，並在完全離線的情況下約60秒內完成完整的5階段管道。這為將AI輔助的胎兒評估與可攜式超聲設備整合建立了一條實用的途徑，直接解決了資源有限環境中的診斷接入差距。代碼、模型和數據可在https://github.com/mahmoodphd/FADA獲得。

##### **PhantomBench: Benchmarking the Non-existential Threat of Language Models**
2606.11105v1 by Haeji Jung, Hila Gonen

Hallucinations, where language models (LMs) generate factually ungrounded responses, pose serious risks, as users tend to blindly rely on them. This is particularly concerning in high-stakes domains, where consequences of such model behavior can lead to significant harms. Despite notable progress in understanding hallucinations, it remains unclear how reliably these models can recognize the limits of their knowledge. We introduce PhantomBench, the first large-scale benchmark of its kind, comprising more than 60K non-existent terms and entities derived from real concepts across diverse domains. Using our benchmark, we evaluate a total of 21 models of various types and sizes. We show staggering hallucination rates across the board (with average rates as high as 86.7% in some cases), and note that even frontier models surprisingly fail to abstain on non-existent concepts, especially when the input presumes their existence. We then show that PhantomBench can serve as a proxy for studying model behavior on rare concepts for which models are more prone to hallucinate. We also provide a pipeline to construct PhantomBench, enabling scalable generation of non-existent concepts tailored to the specific needs of researchers and practitioners.

摘要：幻覺，即語言模型（LMs）生成事實上無根據的回應，帶來了嚴重的風險，因為用戶往往會盲目依賴它們。這在高風險領域尤其令人擔憂，因為這種模型行為的後果可能導致重大損害。儘管在理解幻覺方面取得了顯著進展，但這些模型能多可靠地識別其知識的界限仍然不清楚。我們介紹了 PhantomBench，這是首個此類的大規模基準，包含超過 60K 個不存在的術語和實體，這些術語和實體源自於不同領域的真實概念。利用我們的基準，我們評估了總共 21 種不同類型和大小的模型。我們顯示出驚人的幻覺率（在某些情況下平均高達 86.7%），並指出即使是前沿模型在面對不存在的概念時也令人驚訝地無法避免，特別是當輸入假設它們存在時。我們接著展示了 PhantomBench 可以作為研究模型在稀有概念上的行為的代理，因為模型在這些概念上更容易產生幻覺。我們還提供了一個構建 PhantomBench 的流程，能夠根據研究人員和從業者的具體需求可擴展地生成不存在的概念。

##### **Null-Space Constrained Low-Rank Adaptation for Response-Specified Large Language Model Unlearning**
2606.10989v1 by Bocheng Ju, Jianhua Wang, Chengliang Liu, Xiaolin Chang

Large language model unlearning aims to suppress designated undesirable knowledge while preserving benign capabilities. Many unlearning objectives focus on suppressing undesired answers, while recent target-guided variants specify replacement behavior but still leave update locality largely unconstrained. This paper introduces \emph{Null-Space Constrained Response-Specified Unlearning} (NSRU), a projection-constrained low-rank framework for controlled LLM unlearning. NSRU uses an explicitly structured safe target response to specify the desired behavior for each forget query, while suppressing the original undesired content. To localize adaptation, NSRU estimates per-module retain subspaces from benign hidden representations and uses an orthogonal-projected low-rank parameterization to confine LoRA updates to the null space of the retain subspace. The resulting objective jointly optimizes safe-target learning, undesired-response suppression, and retention preservation under this constrained parameterization. We provide a local first-order analysis showing that the projected update reduces retain-side perturbations while preserving editable directions for shaping forget-query behavior. Experiments on TOFU show that NSRU effectively suppresses extractable forget-set knowledge while improving retain QA performance, model utility, and safe-target alignment over representative baselines. On WMDP, NSRU keeps hazardous-domain accuracy near the random-choice region while preserving broad and domain-adjacent MMLU utility. Ablation studies support the complementary roles of safe-target supervision, undesired-response suppression, retention loss, and null-space projected updates, while sensitivity and robustness analyses indicate stable behavior across the tested hyperparameter and prompt variations.

摘要：大型語言模型的去學習旨在抑制指定的不良知識，同時保留良性的能力。許多去學習目標專注於抑制不希望的答案，而最近的目標導向變體則明確指定替代行為，但仍然在更新的局部性上大致不受限制。本文介紹了\emph{Null-Space Constrained Response-Specified Unlearning}（NSRU），這是一個受限於投影的低秩框架，用於控制大型語言模型的去學習。NSRU使用明確結構的安全目標響應來指定每個遺忘查詢所需的行為，同時抑制原始的不希望內容。為了局部化適應，NSRU從良性的隱藏表示中估計每個模塊的保留子空間，並使用正交投影的低秩參數化將LoRA更新限制在保留子空間的零空間內。由此產生的目標在這一受限參數化下共同優化安全目標學習、不希望的響應抑制和保留保持。我們提供了一個局部的一階分析，顯示投影更新減少了保留側的擾動，同時保留了可編輯的方向以塑造遺忘查詢行為。在TOFU上的實驗表明，NSRU有效地抑制了可提取的遺忘集知識，同時改善了保留問答性能、模型效用和安全目標對齊，相較於代表性基準。在WMDP上，NSRU保持危險領域的準確性接近隨機選擇區域，同時保留廣泛和領域相鄰的MMLU效用。消融研究支持安全目標監督、不希望的響應抑制、保留損失和零空間投影更新的互補角色，而敏感性和穩健性分析則表明在測試的超參數和提示變化下行為穩定。

##### **Provenance Tracking in AI Compilers through the Lens of Coalgebra**
2606.10937v1 by Zilu Tian, Liying Liu

AI compilers aggressively rewrite computation graphs through normalization, lowering, and optimization, making it difficult to track the provenance of tensors and operators across compilation. Reliable provenance is essential for attaching platform-specific postprocessing, debugging compiler behavior, and validating transformations, yet existing solutions are either invasive or ad hoc under non-injective graph rewrites.
  We present a lightweight, generative approach to provenance tracking based on observational semantics. Instead of propagating identifiers through compiler passes, we observe graph transformations and reason about provenance in terms of observable computational actions. We formalize this approach using a coalgebraic model and bisimulation, which preserves provenance even when intermediate nodes are eliminated. Furthermore, we implement this approach in a prototype AI compiler COVAN, demonstrating stable provenance across compilation pipelines with minimal engineering overhead.

摘要：AI 編譯器透過正規化、降低和優化積極重寫計算圖，這使得在編譯過程中追蹤張量和運算子的來源變得困難。可靠的來源追蹤對於附加平台特定的後處理、調試編譯器行為和驗證轉換至關重要，但現有的解決方案在非單射圖重寫下要麼是侵入性的，要麼是臨時的。<lb/>  
我們提出了一種基於觀察語義的輕量級生成方法來進行來源追蹤。與其在編譯器過程中傳播標識符，我們觀察圖變換並根據可觀察的計算行為推理來源。<lb/>  
我們使用共代數模型和雙模擬形式化了這種方法，即使在消除中間節點時也能保留來源。此外，我們在原型 AI 編譯器 COVAN 中實現了這種方法，展示了在編譯管道中以最小的工程開銷實現穩定的來源追蹤。

##### **Trace Only What You Need: Structure-Aware On-Demand Hypergraph Memory for Long-Document Question Answering**
2606.10921v1 by Xiangjun Zai, Xingyu Tan, Chen Chen, Xiaoyang Wang, Wenjie Zhang

Long-document question answering (QA) requires large language models (LLMs) to reason over evidence scattered across lengthy documents, where answers often depend on event order, section-level context, and cross-part evidence connections. Although retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) reduces the input context by retrieving relevant evidence, existing structured RAG methods still face three limitations: costly query-agnostic knowledge organization, insufficient use of original document structure, and no reuse of historical reasoning experience. To address these limitations, we propose DocTrace, a multi-agent RAG framework for long-document QA that supports query-triggered knowledge organization, document-structure-aware and experience-guided reasoning. DocTrace preserves document hierarchy with a lightweight document structural tree index, constructs agent-shared hypergraph-structured working memory on demand during reasoning, and stores successful reasoning plans in graph-structured experience memory for future reuse, enabling adaptive exploration across related long-document questions. Experiments on four long-document QA datasets show that DocTrace achieves the best performance on three datasets, surpassing the strongest baseline, ComoRAG, by up to 8.85% in F1 and 4.40% in EM, while reducing the overall computational cost by 53.32%

摘要：長文問題回答（QA）需要大型語言模型（LLMs）對散布在冗長文檔中的證據進行推理，答案通常依賴於事件順序、部分級上下文和跨部分的證據連結。儘管檢索增強生成（RAG）通過檢索相關證據來減少輸入上下文，但現有的結構化RAG方法仍面臨三個限制：昂貴的查詢無關知識組織、對原始文檔結構的使用不足以及無法重用歷史推理經驗。為了解決這些限制，我們提出了DocTrace，一個支持查詢觸發的知識組織、文檔結構感知和經驗指導推理的多代理RAG框架。DocTrace通過輕量級文檔結構樹索引保留文檔層級，根據需求在推理過程中構建代理共享的超圖結構工作記憶，並將成功的推理計劃存儲在圖結構經驗記憶中以供未來重用，從而實現對相關長文檔問題的自適應探索。在四個長文檔QA數據集上的實驗表明，DocTrace在三個數據集上達到了最佳性能，F1指標超過最強基準ComoRAG達8.85%，EM指標達4.40%，同時將整體計算成本降低了53.32%。

##### **Large-scale semantic mapping of learner agency and autonomy reveals what measurement and generative AI research overlook**
2606.10881v1 by Fei Qin, Xiaobo Liu, Yaowen Zhang, Xuming Li, Fei Wang, Mutlu Cukurova, Jingjing Chen, Yu Zhang

Learner agency and autonomy are foundational to personal development, yet a pervasive "jingle-jangle" fallacy (i.e. identical terms denoting different constructs, distinct terms denoting identical ones) has substantially hindered cumulative knowledge. Treating meaning as a phenomenon constituted through use in linguistic practice, we extracted 8,954 definitions and 2,700 scale items from over 14,000 publications, to investigate how researchers actually used learner agency and autonomy with a semantic analysis pipeline. The definitional landscape of two constructs resolves into three dimensions: regulation and control of learning (task), intrinsic motivation and internal decision-making (person), and social-relational action (sociocultural), thereby empirically quantifying the jingle-jangle fallacy. Existing scales, however, systematically underrepresent the sociocultural dimension. Critically, current generative AI research in education concentrates on learning regulation and control, narrowing the behavioral repertoire that AI-mediated learning environments are designed to cultivate. Beyond conceptual clarification, this work carries direct implications for conceptualization, measurement, and practice towards supporting the multidimensional learner agency and autonomy.

摘要：學習者的能動性和自主性是個人發展的基礎，然而普遍存在的「叮噹-搖鈴」謬誤（即相同的術語表示不同的構念，不同的術語表示相同的構念）實質上阻礙了累積知識。將意義視為通過語言實踐中的使用構成的現象，我們從超過14,000篇出版物中提取了8,954個定義和2,700個量表項目，以調查研究者實際上如何使用學習者的能動性和自主性，並進行語義分析。這兩個構念的定義景觀分解為三個維度：學習的調節和控制（任務）、內在動機和內部決策（個人）以及社會關係行動（社會文化），從而實證量化了叮噹-搖鈴謬誤。然而，現有的量表系統性地低估了社會文化維度。關鍵是，目前在教育領域的生成性人工智慧研究集中於學習的調節和控制，縮小了人工智慧介導的學習環境所設計的行為範疇。除了概念澄清，這項工作對於支持多維度的學習者能動性和自主性在概念化、測量和實踐方面具有直接的影響。

##### **Pushing the Limits of LLM Tool Calling via Experiential Knowledge Integration and Activation**
2606.10875v1 by Yupu Hao, Zhuoran Jin, Huanxuan Liao, Kang Liu, Jun Zhao

Large language models (LLMs) rely on tool use to act as autonomous agents, yet often fail in multi-step execution due to insufficient tool-related knowledge and ineffective knowledge activation. Therefore, we present a systematic study on how knowledge influences tool-use performance, covering the stages of knowledge acquisition, activation, and internalization. In the knowledge acquisition stage, we acquire and evaluate various forms of experiential knowledge, and our analysis shows that simple instance-level knowledge can already provide strong and reliable gains, while abstract intent-level knowledge offers limited benefits. At inference time, to activate knowledge, we find that prompting LLM to expand the depth of reasoning yields diminishing returns, whereas expanding the width of reasoning by parallel sampling with aggregation more effectively activates latent experiential knowledge. At training time, for knowledge internalization, post-training with knowledge-augmented data further improves performance, with reinforcement learning outperforming supervised fine-tuning. Based on these insights, we propose the Knowledge-Augmented Tool Execution (KATE), a knowledge-augmented tool execution framework that integrates experiential knowledge with reasoning-width-expanded inference and knowledge-aware training. Experiments on BFCL-V3 and AppWorld demonstrate consistent and substantial improvements over strong baselines across model scales. Our Code is available at https://github.com/hypasd-art/KATE.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）依賴工具使用來作為自主代理，但由於工具相關知識不足和知識激活不有效，常常在多步執行中失敗。<lb/>因此，我們提出了一項系統性研究，探討知識如何影響工具使用表現，涵蓋知識獲取、激活和內化的階段。<lb/>在知識獲取階段，我們獲取並評估各種形式的經驗知識，我們的分析顯示，簡單的實例級知識已經能提供強大且可靠的增益，而抽象的意圖級知識則提供有限的好處。<lb/>在推理時，為了激活知識，我們發現提示LLM擴展推理的深度會產生遞減的回報，而通過平行取樣和聚合擴展推理的寬度則更有效地激活潛在的經驗知識。<lb/>在訓練時，為了知識內化，使用增強知識的數據進行後訓練進一步提高了性能，強化學習的表現超過了監督微調。<lb/>基於這些見解，我們提出了知識增強工具執行（KATE），這是一個將經驗知識與推理寬度擴展的推理和知識感知訓練相結合的知識增強工具執行框架。<lb/>在BFCL-V3和AppWorld上的實驗顯示，在各模型規模上，相較於強基線有一致且顯著的改進。<lb/>我們的代碼可在 https://github.com/hypasd-art/KATE 獲得。

##### **Attention-Discounted Adaptive Sampler for Masked Diffusion Language Models**
2606.10829v1 by Yusuf Sahin, Ahmed Rockey Saikia, Volkan Cevher, Paolo Favaro

Masked diffusion language models can reduce inference steps by revealing multiple tokens per denoising iteration, but this parallelism is fragile: positions that are individually confident may be unsafe to commit together when their predictions are coupled. Existing training-free samplers such as Top-\(k\), Fast-dLLM, and EB-Sampler mainly control how many tokens to reveal, while often ranking candidates by token-wise scores that ignore interactions within the selected set. We propose ADAS, a training-free reranking rule for parallel masked diffusion decoding. ADAS leaves the base sampler's stopping rule unchanged and modifies only subset construction: it greedily discounts a candidate when it attends strongly to already selected positions whose predictions remain uncertain. Unlike graph-constrained methods that turn attention into hard compatibility constraints, ADAS keeps attention continuous and uses it as a soft marginal penalty. Across LLaDA-8B-Base and Dream-7B-Base on GSM8K, MATH500, HumanEval, and MBPP, plugging ADAS into Top-\(k\), Fast-dLLM, and EB-Sampler improves low-NFE performance at matched denoiser evaluations by \(9.11\) and \(10.46\) percentage points on average, respectively, with \(3.1\%\) per-forward runtime overhead. These results show that soft attention-discounted reranking is a simple and modular way to improve quality in highly parallel decoding for masked diffusion language models.

摘要：被遮蔽的擴散語言模型可以通過每次去噪迭代揭示多個標記來減少推理步驟，但這種並行性是脆弱的：當它們的預測相互關聯時，單獨自信的位置可能不安全一起提交。現有的無需訓練的取樣器，如 Top-\(k\)、Fast-dLLM 和 EB-Sampler 主要控制揭示多少標記，同時通常根據忽略所選集合內部互動的標記分數來排名候選者。我們提出了 ADAS，一種用於並行遮蔽擴散解碼的無需訓練的重新排名規則。ADAS 保持基礎取樣器的停止規則不變，僅修改子集構建：當候選者強烈關注於預測仍然不確定的已選位置時，它會貪婪地折扣該候選者。與將注意力轉化為硬兼容性約束的圖約束方法不同，ADAS 保持注意力的連續性，並將其用作軟邊際懲罰。在 GSM8K、MATH500、HumanEval 和 MBPP 上的 LLaDA-8B-Base 和 Dream-7B-Base 中，將 ADAS 插入 Top-\(k\)、Fast-dLLM 和 EB-Sampler，平均提高了在匹配去噪器評估中的低 NFE 性能 \(9.11\) 和 \(10.46\) 個百分點，並且每次前向運行的開銷為 \(3.1\%\)。這些結果顯示，軟注意力折扣重新排名是一種簡單且模塊化的方式，可以提高遮蔽擴散語言模型的高並行解碼質量。

##### **Earth-OneVision: Extending Remote Sensing Multimodal Large Language Models to More Sensor Modalities and Tasks**
2606.10819v1 by Miaoxin Cai, Guanqun Wang, Wei Zhang, Guangyao Zhou, Yin Zhuang, Tong Zhang, Hao Wang, He Chen, Jun Li

RS-MLLMs enable natural-language understanding and spatial reasoning over earth observation imagery. However, existing models support only a narrow range of sensor types and tasks, yielding a fragmented view of the earth and leaving cross-modal geoscientific knowledge largely unexploited. This work presents Earth-OneVision, a 2B RS-MLLM that unifies six sensor modalities (i.e., optical, SAR, infrared, multispectral, temporal, and video) and cross-sensor fusion across 9 task categories within a single autoregressive framework. Three dedicated mechanisms address three bottlenecks. Full-Granularity Vision-Language Alignment (FGVLA) aligns multi-level visual features with the multi-dimensional language space. Spatial-Linguistic Isomorphic Serialization (SLIS) unifies heterogeneous spatial outputs as autoregressive tokens. Progressive Cross-Modality Adaptation (PCMA) decomposes the compound domain gap into sequential stages, tackling the viewpoint and imaging physics gaps in turn. To support joint training, MMRS-OneVision is constructed with ~34M QA pairs spanning all six sensor modalities and cross-sensor fusion across 9 task categories, substantially exceeding existing RS multimodal instruction datasets. With only 2B parameters, Earth-OneVision achieves competitive or state-of-the-art results across extensive benchmarks, consistently matching or outperforming 4B-72B RS-MLLMs. It achieves 87.52% P@0.5 on the OPT-RSVG testset for optical visual grounding and 80.68% on the SAR VQA benchmark SARLANG-Bench, exceeding 7B models by over 7%. It further achieves 75.74% recall on the BigEarthNet-MS testset for multispectral classification, and 81.94% MCQ accuracy on EarthMind-Bench for cross-modality reasoning.

摘要：RS-MLLMs 使自然語言理解和空間推理能夠應用於地球觀測影像。<lb/>然而，現有模型僅支持有限範圍的傳感器類型和任務，導致對地球的觀察呈現出片段化的視角，並使跨模態地球科學知識大部分未被利用。<lb/>本研究提出了 Earth-OneVision，一個 2B RS-MLLM，統一了六種傳感器模態（即光學、SAR、紅外線、多光譜、時間和視頻）以及在單一自回歸框架內的跨傳感器融合，涵蓋 9 個任務類別。<lb/>三個專門的機制解決了三個瓶頸。<lb/>全粒度視覺-語言對齊（FGVLA）將多層次的視覺特徵與多維語言空間對齊。<lb/>空間-語言同構序列化（SLIS）將異質的空間輸出統一為自回歸標記。<lb/>漸進式跨模態適應（PCMA）將複合領域差距分解為連續階段，依次解決視角和成像物理差距。<lb/>為了支持聯合訓練，MMRS-OneVision 構建了約 3400 萬 QA 對，涵蓋所有六種傳感器模態及 9 個任務類別的跨傳感器融合，顯著超過現有的 RS 多模態指令數據集。<lb/>僅用 2B 參數，Earth-OneVision 在廣泛的基準測試中達到了競爭性或最先進的結果，始終與 4B-72B RS-MLLMs 相匹配或超越。<lb/>在 OPT-RSVG 測試集上，其光學視覺定位達到 87.52% P@0.5，而在 SAR VQA 基準 SARLANG-Bench 上達到 80.68%，超過 7B 模型超過 7%。<lb/>此外，在 BigEarthNet-MS 測試集上，其多光譜分類的召回率達到 75.74%，在 EarthMind-Bench 上的跨模態推理中達到 81.94% 的 MCQ 準確率。

##### **Boosting ECG Classification Performance by Pre-training with Synthesized Data**
2606.10802v1 by Naoki Nonaka, Jun Seita

Deep Neural Networks (DNNs) typically require extensive datasets for effective training. In the medical domain, acquiring large-scale data is often challenging due to privacy concerns and the rarity of certain diseases. To address this data scarcity, we investigate the efficacy of training DNN models using synthetic data, generated based on domain-specific medical knowledge. Specifically, we develop a knowledge-driven Gaussian-composition synthesis algorithm for single-lead II ECGs, in which each heartbeat is represented by Gaussian-shaped P, Q, R, S, and T wave components. Using this simulator, we generate synthetic data for four abnormal electrocardiogram (ECG) classes: atrial fibrillation (AF), atrial flutter (AFLT), premature ventricular complex (PVC), and Wolff-Parkinson-White Syndrome (WPW). We evaluate the utility of this synthetic data by conducting abnormal ECG classification using ten different DNN architectures. Our results demonstrate that synthetic-to-real training improves classification performance for three of the four target abnormalities, with the largest architecture-averaged gain of $33.2\%$ observed for AFLT. Further analysis reveals that the performance enhancement from synthetic data is more pronounced with smaller real-world datasets. These findings suggest that domain-knowledge-based synthetic ECGs can serve as a useful pre-training resource, particularly in scenarios where real-world data are limited or difficult to obtain.

##### **Recovering the Zipfian Distribution in Unsupervised Term Discovery**
2606.10781v1 by Danel Slabbert, Simon Malan, Herman Kamper

Unsupervised term discovery involves segmenting unlabelled speech into word- or syllable-like units and clustering these into a lexicon of candidate types. True lexicons follow a Zipfian distribution, yet the dominant centre-based clustering approach -- K-means -- produces a more uniform distribution due to an inductive bias toward spherical clusters. In this paper we revisit graph-based clustering as a bottom-up alternative, where segment embeddings are connected by pairwise similarity and partitioned using the Leiden algorithm. We show that graph clustering substantially outperforms centre-based approaches (K-means, GMM, BIRCH) in both word- and syllable-level lexicon discovery across three languages, producing more Zipf-like distributions. Another bottom-up approach, agglomerative clustering with average linkage, also performs well, although it is computationally less efficient and allows for less control over the resulting distribution. Our work calls into question the dominance of centre-based clustering for term discovery, and promotes graph clustering as an attractive alternative.

摘要：無監督的術語發現涉及將未標記的語音分割成類似單詞或音節的單位，並將這些單位聚類成候選類型的詞彙表。真正的詞彙表遵循齊夫分佈，然而主導的基於中心的聚類方法——K-means——由於對球形聚類的歸納偏見，產生了更均勻的分佈。在本文中，我們重新審視基於圖的聚類作為一種自下而上的替代方法，其中段落嵌入通過成對相似性連接，並使用Leiden算法進行劃分。我們顯示圖聚類在三種語言的單詞和音節級詞彙發現中，顯著優於基於中心的方法（K-means、GMM、BIRCH），產生了更接近齊夫分佈的結果。另一種自下而上的方法，即使用平均連接的聚合聚類，也表現良好，儘管它在計算上效率較低，並且對最終分佈的控制較少。我們的工作質疑了基於中心的聚類在術語發現中的主導地位，並推廣圖聚類作為一種有吸引力的替代方案。

##### **Detecting Knowledge Gaps from Conversational AI Interactions Using Curriculum Prerequisite Graphs**
2606.10736v1 by Youssef Medhat, Junsoo Park, Ploy Thajchayapong, Ashok K. Goel

Large online courses generate thousands of student questions directed at conversational AI teaching assistants, yet these interaction logs remain largely untapped as diagnostic signals. We present a pipeline that maps student questions from a conversational AI teaching assistant to curriculum topics using a few-shot text classifier, grounded in a GPT-4-extracted prerequisite knowledge graph of course concepts. Evaluated on 1,340 question events from 164 students in a graduate-level AI course, our classifier achieves 80.0% accuracy across 43 labels (42 curriculum topics plus an "unknown" abstention class). Topic-level question volume correlates significantly with student self-reported difficulty from an independent mid-semester survey (rho = 0.491, p = 0.008, n = 28 topics), providing convergent evidence that the classified question stream reflects genuine topic difficulty.
